< review>
#Flashback I was in San Diego, California for 5 months improving my English from February 11 to July 1, 2018. IT was just AMAZING. The city is wonderful, where you can visit a lot of beautiful places and meet a lot of people. I lived in little Italy and went to Converse in Downtown. I had received recommandations from 3 friends who have studied here, and they were right ; It is probably the best school in SD.

First of all, the staff is very friendly and always available. Tamara, the director of the school, is always here if you need help. Joseph, is at the same time the Assistant Academic Manager and an excellent teacher (I was lucky to follow his lessons for 3 months) too. If you have any question, you can ask Heather at the reception, she is always smiling and happy. Sonya is the activities coordinator, thanks to her, I could do skydiving and surfing. She is so sweet !

Finally, Jessica will help you if you want to change classes or lessons. During these 5 months, I definitely improved my English, because of the lesson's quality and the availability of the staff when you want to practice, practice and practice your english :) So don't be shy and talk with them because they could give you a lot of advice about food, places and activities !

For all of the reasons, I definitely recommend you CISL and San Diego. It was the best experience of my life ;¬†I have realized my dream of living in the US for a while,¬†and I don't have regrets, or, maybe yes, just one : I should have stayed more time ! I miss these guys, and I will be back soon to visit them !

See you soon CISL

Anthony Monteleone< /review>

<Review>(Translated by Google) We are French and our children have been participating in the Converse International School of Language junior summer camps for several years. They usually leave for 3 weeks in July and always come back delighted‚Ä¶ with a great American accent. Since 2015, they have stayed at the Washington, Los Angeles, San Francisco and New Haven campuses. The next trip will certainly be to San Diego. I would add that they never wanted to go to the same campus together so as not to be tempted to stay together. On the other hand, during each stay they befriended other young people from all continents and several years later, they still correspond with some.
CISL's programs are well balanced with English classes in the morning and activities in the afternoon. The price of the internships is not excessive because the courses are of high quality, the supervision is very friendly and the accommodation on the university campuses is great. Most importantly, our kids loved going to amusement parks, exploring Hollywood, surfing in Santa Monica, and sightseeing in New York or San Francisco.
In short, at the end of a stay at the ICFTU, the children speak English, learn more about American culture and have had the best vacation of their lives. A great experience!

Last clarification: for those under 15 who are traveling as Unaccompanied minors with Air France, Converse sends a manager to the airport to pick up the young person on arrival. For the others a taxi awaits them. Everything is planned!

<rating>5< /rating>< review>
These people are great!  Smiling, professional faces from the moment you walk in the door.  The Doctors and FNP's AND the Dentists are friendly, caring, professionals.  When you have visited them you know you are getting the best care possible.

Plus, they have a BRAND NEW facility with all the latest equipment of modern health care.

The fact that they provide BOTH Medical care AND Dental care at the same location is really great.

Another GREAT thing about them is that they work on a sliding scale for lower income Seniors and other financially distressed persons and families.  No need to fear unreasonable Medical bills here.  Where else can you get a cavity filled for $50?  Awesome for a disabled Senior!

I moved from a Family Practice down the street that is failing.  I had to wait a while to get on the patient roll, but well worth the wait!

Also, my FNP, Dana Underwood, is one of the best I have encountered.  She is caring, informed, thorough and puts your needs above all else.  No repeated watching the clock to see how soon they can move on to the next patient here!  If there are issues that take a bit more time, you get the attention.  If it is just a check-up, that's good too...

So, in conclusion, THANKS YOU ALL FOR YOUR KIND AND AWESOME HEALTH CARE!</review>

<date>1564876236705</date><Rating>5</Rating><text>OK, I grew up on the east coast, Boston to be exact. Yo they bake their rolls daily here, they got that peppercini, classic oil and vinegar. I went here yesterday after just moving back to CA from Boston. If I'm in OB, I WILL be going to Lu's no matter what. They also have a bomb dessert selection, great drinks, indoor and outdoor seating, and the staff is as friendly as your best friend, and they mean it. If I could rate 6 stars, you can bet Lu's would get it. This place basically changed my view on the lack of east coast sub-style food in San Diego. I'm really relieved to know this place exists. So ya, it's that kinda seriously good.</text><pics>None</pics>< response>

<text>I came here purposely to try out the Amaretti cookies. My sister LOVES these type of cookies and there were reviews on Yelp that they make them here. I came here and  bought 5 of them ($1 a piece - a bit pricey for the size of the cookie) and 2 wedding cookies. They did have sandwiches too that looked appealing but I did not get any at this time. < text>
Easily the Best cannoli in town! These guys not only make their own cannoli shells but the ricotta cream filling is this ultra tasty, whipped to perfection cream that you just can't stop eating. All the other sweet treats are no less impressive. Many types of cookies and all of them fresh and uncompromisingly delicious. Definitely try the macaroons and the chocolate dipped cookies.
On the sandwich side they make spectacular subs, mostly with traditional Italian ingredients, some of them toasted. I just had the eggplants and mozzarella sammy and it's an instant favorite.
There is some outside seating, so you can enjoy your lunch/dessert without delay.
A great contribution to the neighborhood.</text>

<review>Let me just start by saying I am VERY PICKY about who does my hair.  I have switched stylists many times over the last few years.  I've been to a few in downtown SD, some in  Fancy Schmancy- La Jolla, and all over North County and paid way too much for my highlights, I've tried numerous AVEDA salons, and then continued on my quest to find a great colorist, but I have finally ended my search after I met Freddy.

The Salon is very cute and trendy too, it's in downtown SD and plays great music.  They also serve fun drinks and keep you entertained while you wait.

< Text>
Olivier and the team were great. I had a diagnostic done at the dealership for my check engine light while my car was in for an unrelated recall. Dealership prices are astronomical, so I called Pacific Auto, who quoted me less than half the cost for the same repairs. They got me in the next day and even redid the diagnostic to double check before they started repairs. Turns out, the dealership was wrong and my radiator wasn't leaking, the hose connection was just loose. They did the other repairs necessary and retightened the hose fitting. All in all, they saved me $1400+ compared to the dealership and had my car back to me the next day.  They're honest with what needs to be done, quick, and very affordable. I wouldn't hesitate to bring my car back for future repairs.</Text>

<Text>The positives:
The maintenance crew is top notch (Igor and Alex are 5 star employees). Any requests are taken care of promptly. In addition, the community is safe, overall pretty quiet, lots of parking, packages are delivered straight to your door, and a 10-15 minute walk to the Caltrain station and downtown Sunnyvale. The apartment units themselves look nice considering the buildings are older and have lots of storage and/or closet space. Before Covid-19, the pool area was beautiful and relaxing, there were grills to use, and the fitness room had great basic equipment.

The negatives:
The units themselves could use a lot of upgrades. My fridge and AC both stopped working and had to be replaced - it would be nice if they could invest in energy efficient appliances. The units aren't sound proof; luckily my neighbors have been quiet individuals, but even a normal volume conversation can sound like an echo from above or below you. New renters should avoid any units facing the train tracks (Buildings 100 and 120) otherwise you will be in for a surprise when one particular freight train rolls through each night between 9pm-midnight and shakes your whole building. They had people come do balcony "repair" work across all units, but the repairs looked no different than what it looked previously.

The ultra negative:
Obviously, the pandemic has resulted in the pool area only being for swimming (no lounge chairs), the grills closed off, and the fitness room closed. While unfortunate, this is understandable, but only up until a new lease rolls around and Equity Residential gives a lease "offer" renewal of the same as what we signed pre Covid-19. What...? Do they want us to say we are grateful for not raising our rate 10% like they normally do? The process of trying to negotiate down is like pulling teeth, and Equity Residential will take over a week to respond to emails, and will provide another "offer" that is still way above market rate (and way above what they are asking on the SAME OR LARGER available units at Briarwood) and say the "offer" is only valid for 24 hours. What? (I'm looking at you, Amber Pardue on the Corporate Renewals team, and whoever your 'negations' boss is). The worst part is that I've been at Briarwood since June 2018 and have lived in 3 different units within 2.5 years. This is because larger units will be available and less expensive than the renewal "offers", yet Equity Residential would rather have me transfer to a unit down the sidewalk every year than allow me to continue living at my current (now former) unit for a reasonable market rate price. If it sounds like it doesn't make sense, that's because it doesn't. Oh, and my counteroffer that Equity Residential rejected? My old apartment is listed as available on their website for a monthly rate $150 LOWER than my counteroffer (and listed over $700 less per month than their renewal offer to me). Please, remind me how I'm a "valued resident"?? Because I don't feel like one.< /Text>< rate>

<GmapID>0x808fb6f8582dfa2b:0x112c02633d177f3b< /GmapID>< review>
So I generally do not write reviews but I really HAVE to this time. I have been a resident at the Briarwood Apartments, Sunnyvale for close to 5 years now.
Unfortunately, I have decided to move up north towards San Francisco for personal reasons. But, I need to let the world know, that this gem of an apartment complex (with a gem of a manager, more on her later) in the heart of Sunnyvale is an amazing place to live. If you work at WalmartLabs, then this should be your default apartment of choice. It is close to 101, and 280, you can walk to the Caltrain station, and to the historic murphy avenue (Sunnyvale downtown) with plenty of food and drink options. The location is central, yet the apartment complex is extremely peaceful. The residents are nice and courteous and the complex is clean. Plenty of large parking spaces and a new and amazing gym. Regular food trucks and a beautiful pool. I have loved every minute I have spent here. And now, the star of the review, Suree Marley. I don‚Äôt have words to describe this amazing person. She is extremely kind and is always ready to help. I kept running to her for something or the other, and she will always hear me out patiently and will always help me in the greatest possible manner. It is a shame that she will not be my property manager anymore, but Hey Equity, the only reason I picked my next equity apartment is because you have people like Suree. I will miss her a lot. One more person I need to talk about is Igor. What and honest and sincere man. Hats off to you Igor. Many years ago in 2014, he refused to accept a tip from me because he said it is his duty to help me. Briarwood apartment is an amazing place (with an amazing team) to call home and I would always cherish the time I have spent here.</review>

<date>1483994574407< /date><Rating>2</Rating>< Review>
Lived here for the last 2 years before moving out last month.
Initially the experience was pleasant - seemingly good location, relatively affordable rent, quiet neighbors, and Chantel in the leasing office was fantastic. However, once she left the complex in early 2015, everything went downhill. The staff never warned that Caltrain would be SO loud and would go by so fast that it produced mini earthquakes that shook all the walls of my apartment every day.
Eventually incredibly obnoxious neighbors moved in all around us - blasting music at all hours, dogs barking 24/7, and my favorite - constantly screaming infants! The grandparents would bring the infants out onto the balcony when they started crying/screaming so everyone and their mother in the complex could hear it, regardless of what time it was...kill me now! So inconsiderate! Had to call the cops more than once on a few neighbors.
When I first moved in, the maintenance staff told me that they were short one cabinet for my kitchen and promised to get it to me right away. Yet 2 years later, still no cabinet! Instead of continuing to ask repeatedly for the cabinet, my roommate put a print out of a "This is where I'd put a cabinet...IF I HAD ONE!" meme on the wall in its place.
On top of that, the seal of our refrigerator broke about 8 months ago. When my roommate went to the office to ask for a repair, explaining that we hadn't been able to buy milk for 6 months since it didn't stay cold in the refrigerator, a member of the leasing staff said‚Ä¶and I directly quote..."well, just drink it [the milk] faster..."! That was it! Not "oh so sorry, let us fix it for you"...just "drink it faster..." - SERIOUSLY?!   So we said, we see your rent increase and attitude, we're out of here! For the astronomical cost of rent they charge to keep up with the newer Silicon Valley complexes, you‚Äôd think they‚Äôd be more diligent about renovating/maintaining the place.
For all the gripes I might have with this complex and the people who live there, I will say that as we approached the tail end of our lease, Alyssa in the leasing office was a bright spot. She was always very helpful, pleasant, and professional. She even brought my packages from the leasing office to my front door when she got off work, which was pretty convenient seeing as how her apartment was just around the corner from my unit, and very much appreciated as I did not usually get home from work until well after the leasing office closed.< /Review>

<rating>5< /rating><Review>We eat at el castillito once a week and i have been eating there for almost 2 decades now.

I consider it to be one of the top 3 taquerias in san francisco.

In my opinion they have the best al pastor (marinated pork) in the entire city.

The super meat burrito is substantial enough that we often split one between 2 people.

The super tacos are the perfect lunch/afternoon snack.

We live around the corner but i often go there to sit at the window and people watch while having tacos.

Some people may also like how they ask you the type of beans, rice and other fillings right there as they are making it in front of you.

My recommendation (careful as this is mucho caliente): regular meat burrito with al pastor, black beans, spicy salsa, everything on it, extra jalalenos, extra salsa roja.

The chips are not the best in the city but they are good enough. The salsa bar has the basics.</Review><pictures>None< /pictures>< response>

< Review>
Probably one of the better taquerias in this area of town. The beef and the chicken are fantastic. I want the pork to be good given the tasty spit they have hanging but unfortunately it is dry :(. Burritos are huge, their  tacos are also of large size for a relatively reasonable price. The torta is an interesting little bit worth getting but probably also worth splitting with someone since it is huge. All and all this place is a great place to get the Mission fix outside of the Mission.</Review>

<userid>117646993640195336681<//userid>< user_name>
Bernard K<//user_name>
<Date>1534923819204< /Date><Rate>5</Rate>< text>
This is the type of Mexican restaurant that will make every New Yorker stop dead in their tracks. Unassuming. Rugged. Authentic. It's the type of cuisine you'd expect to only find in the depths of Parts Unknown, but allas here we are in the center of it all, San Francisco.

This isn't your grandma's ricearoni joint. This is straight up south of the border home cooking. Every man has his vice. At El Castillito, expertly named for a famous castle, I found mine...the vegetarian burrito.

Ordering from the man behind the counter repping the SF Giants hat, I can tell he is ready for business...he is ready to serve up the burrito that will make my night. Assertive, yet attentive, he asks me to make some of the hardest choices of the evening. Black beans or pinto beans? Cilantro? You get the drill. Once the bad boy is all wrapped up, he gives it another 30 seconds on the oven to heat up to a perfected crisp. Perfection at last.

After paying what is due, I make sure to grab some salsas and slather my burrito up. It's time to induldge. The crescendo of the evening is finally here. I take the first bite, the salsa verde hitting my palate doesn't hold back. Excellence. They don't make it this good in NYC. The first bite, game over. This is it. Satisfaction at long last. And I still have the entire burrito to go.

If you're in the neighborhood, try El Castillito. You won't be disappointed. And if you are, it's definitely you.< /text>

Probably one of the better taquerias in this area of town. The beef and the chicken are fantastic. I want the pork to be good given the tasty spit they have hanging but unfortunately it is dry :(. <Resp>None<//Resp><Text>Get the green tomatillo sauce. I don't care if you're only there for a glass of freshly made (squeezed? pressed?) carrot juice: get the green tomatillo sauce. It is just creamy and just spicy enough to be the perfect complement to any item on the menu at El Castillito.

The quesadilla el castillito (con pollo o carne asada) is a perennial favorite and a worthy vessel for the green tomatillo salsa. The friendly cook always tricks me into speaking Spanish, and I oblige up until he asks me what kind of beans I want with my quesadilla and I have to say, "Frijoles...uh...refried-o".

Another secret is the vegetable burrito, which you can pair with the green tomatillo sauce. The vegetable burrito is packed with grilled veggies and is both cheaper and tastier than the plain bean and rice business that is the vegetarian burrito.

You can ask for chips at the cash register. I always do because eating chips dipped in green tomatillo salsa is normal and drinking a cup of green tomatillo salsa neat is not.< /Text><date>1414449078953<//date>< gmapID>
